[/wiki/Lausanne] (building on the right side of this photo)Logitech International S.A. (/ˈlɒdʒɪtɛk/ [/wiki/Help:IPA/English]; commonly referred to as Logitech or Logi; stylized as logitech,
previously LOGITECH) is a Swiss [/wiki/Switzerland] provider of personal computer [/wiki/Personal_computer] and mobile
accessories, with its headquarters in Lausanne [/wiki/Lausanne], Switzerland and administrative headquarters in Newark
[/wiki/Newark,_California], California [/wiki/California]. In addition to its Swiss and American facilities, the company has
offices throughout Europe, Asia and the rest of the Americas. Logitech's sales and marketing activities are organized into three
geographic regions: Americas (AMR); Europe, Middle East and Africa (EMEA); Asia Pacific (AP).

The company develops and markets personal peripherals for PC navigation, video communication and collaboration, music and smart
homes. This includes products like keyboards [/wiki/Computer_keyboard], mice [/wiki/Computer_mouse], tablet
[/wiki/Tablet_computer] accessories, webcams [/wiki/Webcam], Bluetooth speakers, universal remotes [/wiki/Universal_remote] and
more.

The name Logitech is derived from the French word for software, "logiciel".[3] In Japan, Logitech was established as Logicool to
avoid conflict with the Logitec brand.

[//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png]
[/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg]This section relies too much on references [/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability] to primary sources. 
Please improve this section by adding secondary or tertiary sources. (January 2018) (Learn how and when to remove this template
message [/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal])Logitech International S.A. was co-founded in Apples, Vaud [/wiki/Apples,_Vaud], Switzerland, in 1981 by two Stanford
[/wiki/Stanford] alumni, Daniel Borel [/wiki/Daniel_Borel] and Pierluigi Zappacosta [/wiki/Pierluigi_Zappacosta], and a former 
Olivetti [/wiki/Olivetti] engineer, Giacomo Marini [/wiki/Giacomo_Marini].[4]

For a time during its formative years, Logitech's Silicon Valley [/wiki/Silicon_Valley] offices occupied space at 165 University
Avenue [/wiki/165_University_Avenue], Palo Alto [/wiki/Palo_Alto], California [/wiki/California], home to a number of noted
technology startups.[5]

In 2007, Logitech licensed Hillcrest Labs [/wiki/Hillcrest_Labs]' Freespace motion control technology to produce the MX Air Mouse,
which allows a user to use natural gestures to control a PC.[6][7]

In August 2008, Logitech acquired Ultimate Ears, supplier of custom in-ear monitors for professional musicians and earphones for
the consumer market.[8]

In December 2008, Logitech announced that it had manufactured one billion mice since 1985.[9]

In July 2011, Logitech acquired the mobile visual communications provider, Mirial [/wiki/Mirial_s.u.r.l.].[10]

In January 2013, Bracken Darrell became Logitech’s chief executive officer and then CEO Guerrino De Luca continued as Logitech’s
chairman of the board.[11]

In April 2016, Logitech agreed to pay US$7.5 million penalty related to accusations that it and some former executives improperly
inflated the company's results for its 2011 fiscal year to meet guidance and other accounting violations. The U.S. Securities and
Exchange Commission said the alleged accounting issues left investors without an accurate view of the Swiss-U.S. company's
finances.[12]

On September 15, 2016, Logitech announced that they had purchased the Saitek [/wiki/Saitek] brand and assets from Mad Catz
[/wiki/Mad_Catz] for US$13 million in cash.[13]

On August 11, 2017, Logitech acquired ASTRO Gaming, makers of professional gaming equipment (mainly headset solutions), for US$85
million in cash.[14]

PRODUCTION[EDIT [/W/INDEX.PHP?TITLE=LOGITECH&ACTION=EDIT&SECTION=2]]
The first Logitech mice were made in Le Lieu [/wiki/Le_Lieu], in the Swiss Canton of Vaud [/wiki/Canton_of_Vaud] by Dubois Depraz
SA.[citation needed [/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed]]

Production facilities were then established in the US [/wiki/United_States], Taiwan [/wiki/Taiwan], Hungary [/wiki/Hungary] and 
Ireland [/wiki/Ireland] before being moved to Suzhou [/wiki/Suzhou], China. As of 2005[update]
[//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Logitech&action=edit], the manufacturing operations in China produce approximately half of
Logitech's products. The remaining production is outsourced to contract manufacturers [/wiki/Contract_manufacturer] and original
design manufacturers in Asia [/wiki/Asia].[citation needed [/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed]]

LOGITECH PRODUCT LINES[EDIT [/W/INDEX.PHP?TITLE=LOGITECH&ACTION=EDIT&SECTION=3]]
 * Logitech [/wiki/List_of_Logitech_products] – worldwide (except in Japan [/wiki/Japan], where it is known as Logicool) for PC 
   peripherals [/wiki/Peripheral], remote controls [/wiki/Remote_control_handset], security cameras [/wiki/Security_camera], mice
   [/wiki/Mouse_(computing)], keyboards [/wiki/Computer_keyboard], webcams [/wiki/Webcam], Computer speakers
   [/wiki/Computer_speaker], and accessories for smart phones and tablet keyboards and covers
 * Logitech video collaboration, including all B2B video conferencing equipment
 * Logitech MX - computer accessories (mice)
 * Logitech G gaming [/wiki/Video_games] products. Called Logicool G in Japan.
 * LifeSize [/wiki/LifeSize] – video conferencing [/wiki/Video_conferencing] products
 * Ultimate Ears [/wiki/Ultimate_Ears] (UE) - in-ear monitors [/wiki/In-ear_monitor], wireless Bluetooth [/wiki/Bluetooth] 
   Speakers and universal-fit earphones [/wiki/Earphone]
 * Jaybird [/wiki/Jaybird_(company)] for wireless bluetooth sport earbuds
 * Slim Devices [/wiki/Slim_Devices] audio brand
 * Saitek [/wiki/Saitek] - purchased on 15 September 2016, from Mad Catz [/wiki/Mad_Catz]
 * Logitech Harmony [/wiki/Logitech_Harmony] programmable remote controls

PRODUCT DESCRIPTION 
Style Name:Z333 PRODUCT DESCRIPTION


Powerful sound, deep bass. Logitech Multimedia Speakers Z333 deliver 80 W of powerful and immersive acoustics that are crisp,
clear and balanced. The front-facing subwoofer with a 13 cm (5 inch) driver produces a deep bass response, adding intensity to
your music, movies and games. Adjust bass via the bass control knob and easily command your sound using the wired control pod,
which allows access to power and volume. 3.5 mm + RCA inputs allow you to connect almost any device with an audio output, such as
a computer, tablet, smartphone - or even a TV.

 * 80 W peak power (40 W RMS)
 *  Front-facing subwoofer with 13-cm (5 inch) driver for deep, rich bass
 * Wired control pod for easy access to power and volume
 * Dedicated control knob to adjust bass
 *  Headphone jack
 *  3.5 mm + RCA connectivity inputs





BOX CONTAINS
Two satellite speakers
Subwoofer
User documentation
2-year manufacturer's guarantee and full product support.

First impressions:
They sound great!! my bedroom is currently bouncing and i dont even have the volume half way and the sub isnt even maxed out. it
has great potential to annoy the neighbors.

Packaging:
I highly recommend you have a knife to cut the outer box open and a pair of scissors to remove it from the packaging, the cables
were all tightly packed in so to reduce the stress on cables use scissors and gently cut them out of the packaging i'm hoping that
the care I've taken to get them out of the box prevents me from ruining into the same situation others have of them not working a
few months down the line. other than that package was in perfect condition.

The setup:
It was quite simple to set up i plugged everything in before given it power. I really can appreciate how it sounds at under half
volume so i dont really need MAX power, i hope these will last a very long time hoping for 5 or more years out of them so I'm
going to be careful on how i use them. the cables are long enough the volume thing has a very long cable 2 metres i guess got it
on the opposite side to the subwoofer on my desk so i can easily reach it and the cable that goes into my pc that's fed through
the back of the desk so that's long enough too.

Gaming:
it sounds good for gaming too however i prefer the directional sound that i get from my turtle beach 450 7.1 surroundsound
headset. its still a good speaker set though.

So far im extremely impressed with how music sounds and happy with this purchase.

really really good, but be prepared to have the woofer very close to your feet because of short wires. The sound is great. Not
_wonderful_, no breathtaking bass (according to some tests i ran bass sound becomes audible from around 60Hz) but, hey!, very good
still. The bluetooth thing is great, while it only saves you one wired connection (at the expense of having a wire from woofer to
the volume control), it still is really great not having to hook up any cables to my laptop/mobile.

wire for each speaker would be good. And the volume control should not be fixed to the woofer - this is my reason for not giving
full five stars. I'd like to have the woofer in another corner of the room - I could buy extension cables for the speakers, but

I use these speakers on my tablet for watching Youtube videos and listening to Spotify with the Aux cable plugged in.
The problem is that when your video or song ends, the Aux, from the logitech, shuts off and you get a terrible buzz, even when the
Aux is still plugged in. As soon as you give it a signal again, the buzz goes, but if you have it plugged in to a tablet or phone
or any mini jack, if you don't feed it a single it will buzz. The louder you have the speakers the louder the buzz, so to combat
this make sure your volume is up full on your device, so you don't have to have the speakers so loud, this means the buzz will be
quieter, still annoying though, really annoying!

This is a really annoying little fault.Read more [javascript:void(0)]Comment|2 people found this helpful. Was this review helpful
to you? Yes

ABOUT LOGITECH G27
Racing wheel and pedal sets are a popular accessory for players that enjoy motor racing video games, and the Logitech G27 is
designed to replicate the real-life driving experience with a number of features that would be found in a regular car. This
particular model is targeted at PC and PS3 owners, and it comes as three separate units - the wheel and steering column, the gear
shift and pedals. Materials such as Stainless Steel, bearings and leather have been used in the design to make the whole setup
long-lasting. While traditional steering wheel products have always handled like a regular joystick, the Logitech G27 includes
force feedback, and this provides resistance for the steering wheel to replicate the feeling of tyres losing grip on the road. RPM
indicator LED lights allow experienced video game drivers to have full control over gear shift changes when driving in manual
mode, and this can help players to gain a vital speed advantage during a race. As the Logitech G27 comes in three distinct pieces,
accessories are available that allow owners to arrange the parts so that the arrangement is laid out like a real car. Stands make
it easier to choose a left-hand drive or right-hand layout, and custom pedal modifications can also be found that give a more
realistic feeling when pressing down on the accelerator, clutch and brake. For the dedicated video game racing enthusiast,
complete solutions are available, including a racing chair and stand - this provides a complete internal vehicle environment.

[/wiki/Lausanne] (building on the right side of this photo)Logitech International S.A. (/ˈlɒdʒɪtɛk/ [/wiki/Help:IPA/English]; commonly referred to as Logitech or Logi; stylized as logitech,
previously LOGITECH) is a Swiss [/wiki/Switzerland] provider of personal computer [/wiki/Personal_computer] and mobile
accessories, with its headquarters in Lausanne [/wiki/Lausanne], Switzerland and administrative headquarters in Newark
[/wiki/Newark,_California], California [/wiki/California]. In addition to its Swiss and American facilities, the company has
offices throughout Europe, Asia and the rest of the Americas. Logitech's sales and marketing activities are organized into three
geographic regions: Americas (AMR); Europe, Middle East and Africa (EMEA); Asia Pacific (AP).

The company develops and markets personal peripherals for PC navigation, video communication and collaboration, music and smart
homes. This includes products like keyboards [/wiki/Computer_keyboard], mice [/wiki/Computer_mouse], tablet
[/wiki/Tablet_computer] accessories, webcams [/wiki/Webcam], Bluetooth speakers, universal remotes [/wiki/Universal_remote] and
more.

The name Logitech is derived from the French word for software, "logiciel".[3] In Japan, Logitech was established as Logicool to
avoid conflict with the Logitec brand.

[//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png]
[/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg]This section relies too much on references [/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability] to primary sources. 
Please improve this section by adding secondary or tertiary sources. (January 2018) (Learn how and when to remove this template
message [/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal])Logitech International S.A. was co-founded in Apples, Vaud [/wiki/Apples,_Vaud], Switzerland, in 1981 by two Stanford
[/wiki/Stanford] alumni, Daniel Borel [/wiki/Daniel_Borel] and Pierluigi Zappacosta [/wiki/Pierluigi_Zappacosta], and a former 
Olivetti [/wiki/Olivetti] engineer, Giacomo Marini [/wiki/Giacomo_Marini].[4]

For a time during its formative years, Logitech's Silicon Valley [/wiki/Silicon_Valley] offices occupied space at 165 University
Avenue [/wiki/165_University_Avenue], Palo Alto [/wiki/Palo_Alto], California [/wiki/California], home to a number of noted
technology startups.[5]

In 2007, Logitech licensed Hillcrest Labs [/wiki/Hillcrest_Labs]' Freespace motion control technology to produce the MX Air Mouse,
which allows a user to use natural gestures to control a PC.[6][7]

In August 2008, Logitech acquired Ultimate Ears, supplier of custom in-ear monitors for professional musicians and earphones for
the consumer market.[8]

In December 2008, Logitech announced that it had manufactured one billion mice since 1985.[9]

In July 2011, Logitech acquired the mobile visual communications provider, Mirial [/wiki/Mirial_s.u.r.l.].[10]

In January 2013, Bracken Darrell became Logitech’s chief executive officer and then CEO Guerrino De Luca continued as Logitech’s
chairman of the board.[11]

In April 2016, Logitech agreed to pay US$7.5 million penalty related to accusations that it and some former executives improperly
inflated the company's results for its 2011 fiscal year to meet guidance and other accounting violations. The U.S. Securities and
Exchange Commission said the alleged accounting issues left investors without an accurate view of the Swiss-U.S. company's
finances.[12]

On September 15, 2016, Logitech announced that they had purchased the Saitek [/wiki/Saitek] brand and assets from Mad Catz
[/wiki/Mad_Catz] for US$13 million in cash.[13]

On August 11, 2017, Logitech acquired ASTRO Gaming, makers of professional gaming equipment (mainly headset solutions), for US$85
million in cash.[14]

PRODUCTION[EDIT [/W/INDEX.PHP?TITLE=LOGITECH&ACTION=EDIT&SECTION=2]]
The first Logitech mice were made in Le Lieu [/wiki/Le_Lieu], in the Swiss Canton of Vaud [/wiki/Canton_of_Vaud] by Dubois Depraz
SA.[citation needed [/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed]]

Production facilities were then established in the US [/wiki/United_States], Taiwan [/wiki/Taiwan], Hungary [/wiki/Hungary] and 
Ireland [/wiki/Ireland] before being moved to Suzhou [/wiki/Suzhou], China. As of 2005[update]
[//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Logitech&action=edit], the manufacturing operations in China produce approximately half of
Logitech's products. The remaining production is outsourced to contract manufacturers [/wiki/Contract_manufacturer] and original
design manufacturers in Asia [/wiki/Asia].[citation needed [/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed]]

LOGITECH PRODUCT LINES[EDIT [/W/INDEX.PHP?TITLE=LOGITECH&ACTION=EDIT&SECTION=3]]
 * Logitech [/wiki/List_of_Logitech_products] – worldwide (except in Japan [/wiki/Japan], where it is known as Logicool) for PC 
   peripherals [/wiki/Peripheral], remote controls [/wiki/Remote_control_handset], security cameras [/wiki/Security_camera], mice
   [/wiki/Mouse_(computing)], keyboards [/wiki/Computer_keyboard], webcams [/wiki/Webcam], Computer speakers
   [/wiki/Computer_speaker], and accessories for smart phones and tablet keyboards and covers
 * Logitech video collaboration, including all B2B video conferencing equipment
 * Logitech MX - computer accessories (mice)
 * Logitech G gaming [/wiki/Video_games] products. Called Logicool G in Japan.
 * LifeSize [/wiki/LifeSize] – video conferencing [/wiki/Video_conferencing] products
 * Ultimate Ears [/wiki/Ultimate_Ears] (UE) - in-ear monitors [/wiki/In-ear_monitor], wireless Bluetooth [/wiki/Bluetooth] 
   Speakers and universal-fit earphones [/wiki/Earphone]
 * Jaybird [/wiki/Jaybird_(company)] for wireless bluetooth sport earbuds
 * Slim Devices [/wiki/Slim_Devices] audio brand
 * Saitek [/wiki/Saitek] - purchased on 15 September 2016, from Mad Catz [/wiki/Mad_Catz]
 * Logitech Harmony [/wiki/Logitech_Harmony] programmable remote controls

PRODUCT DESCRIPTION 
Style Name:Z333 PRODUCT DESCRIPTION


Powerful sound, deep bass. Logitech Multimedia Speakers Z333 deliver 80 W of powerful and immersive acoustics that are crisp,
clear and balanced. The front-facing subwoofer with a 13 cm (5 inch) driver produces a deep bass response, adding intensity to
your music, movies and games. Adjust bass via the bass control knob and easily command your sound using the wired control pod,
which allows access to power and volume. 3.5 mm + RCA inputs allow you to connect almost any device with an audio output, such as
a computer, tablet, smartphone - or even a TV.

 * 80 W peak power (40 W RMS)
 *  Front-facing subwoofer with 13-cm (5 inch) driver for deep, rich bass
 * Wired control pod for easy access to power and volume
 * Dedicated control knob to adjust bass
 *  Headphone jack
 *  3.5 mm + RCA connectivity inputs





BOX CONTAINS
Two satellite speakers
Subwoofer
User documentation
2-year manufacturer's guarantee and full product support.

MR JJ McGuire [/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AEZ4NJW3UP6IMREOK3IIDWSUZLNQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_gw_tr?ie=UTF8]5.0 out of 5 stars
[/gp/customer-reviews/R1FQ7F7L1YQ2Z/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]Lovely sound Quality
[/gp/customer-reviews/R1FQ7F7L1YQ2Z/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]28 September 2017Style: Z333|Verified Purchase
First impressions:
They sound great!! my bedroom is currently bouncing and i dont even have the volume half way and the sub isnt even maxed out. it
has great potential to annoy the neighbors.

Packaging:
I highly recommend you have a knife to cut the outer box open and a pair of scissors to remove it from the packaging, the cables
were all tightly packed in so to reduce the stress on cables use scissors and gently cut them out of the packaging i'm hoping that
the care I've taken to get them out of the box prevents me from ruining into the same situation others have of them not working a
few months down the line. other than that package was in perfect condition.

The setup:
It was quite simple to set up i plugged everything in before given it power. I really can appreciate how it sounds at under half
volume so i dont really need MAX power, i hope these will last a very long time hoping for 5 or more years out of them so I'm
going to be careful on how i use them. the cables are long enough the volume thing has a very long cable 2 metres i guess got it
on the opposite side to the subwoofer on my desk so i can easily reach it and the cable that goes into my pc that's fed through
the back of the desk so that's long enough too.

Gaming:
it sounds good for gaming too however i prefer the directional sound that i get from my turtle beach 450 7.1 surroundsound
headset. its still a good speaker set though.

So far im extremely impressed with how music sounds and happy with this purchase.

Update: (Will update if i need to add anything or something changes)
1. ive had a week of using them now ok its early days but still sounding great no problems at all if your wondering then i aint
using wireless its all plugged in with cables, ive turned them up a little bit too they must be extremely loud at full volume i
doubt ill ever have to go to the max when i say they got power i mean THEY GOT POWER!!!! Bass boosted music will make your house
shake and most likely have the neighbors calling the cops on you they so freakin LOUD!!! best pc speakers ive ever had. hope they
last a long time.Read more [javascript:void(0)]Comment|7 people found this helpful. Was this review helpful to you? Yes

[/gp/customer-reviews/R2NRYZ8YCZ90GT/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]really good sound quality in this price range
[/gp/customer-reviews/R2NRYZ8YCZ90GT/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]29 January 2018Style: Z337|Verified Purchase
really really good, but be prepared to have the woofer very close to your feet because of short wires. The sound is great. Not
_wonderful_, no breathtaking bass (according to some tests i ran bass sound becomes audible from around 60Hz) but, hey!, very good
still. The bluetooth thing is great, while it only saves you one wired connection (at the expense of having a wire from woofer to
the volume control), it still is really great not having to hook up any cables to my laptop/mobile.

For the price I think this product is almost worth full five stars, except for the length of the cables. A bit too short. I know,
if they were longer I (or someone else) would probably complain of cables being too long... I just think that an extra foot of
wire for each speaker would be good. And the volume control should not be fixed to the woofer - this is my reason for not giving
full five stars. I'd like to have the woofer in another corner of the room - I could buy extension cables for the speakers, but
the volume control is on a fixed short cable and that would then have to be somewhere near the woofer, and I have no means of
extending that.Read more [javascript:void(0)]Comment|3 people found this helpful. Was this review helpful to you? Yes

PMunkus [/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AF5RSTL2STMMQUXMAMDOHWIKHNJA/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_gw_tr?ie=UTF8]3.0 out of 5 stars
[/gp/customer-reviews/R1UTBZ8LHIS2NY/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]Buzz Aldrin!
[/gp/customer-reviews/R1UTBZ8LHIS2NY/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]16 February 2018Style: Z333|Verified Purchase
As multimedia speakers these are great, but they do have one massive draw back.
I use these speakers on my tablet for watching Youtube videos and listening to Spotify with the Aux cable plugged in.
The problem is that when your video or song ends, the Aux, from the logitech, shuts off and you get a terrible buzz, even when the
Aux is still plugged in. As soon as you give it a signal again, the buzz goes, but if you have it plugged in to a tablet or phone
or any mini jack, if you don't feed it a single it will buzz. The louder you have the speakers the louder the buzz, so to combat
this make sure your volume is up full on your device, so you don't have to have the speakers so loud, this means the buzz will be
quieter, still annoying though, really annoying!

This is a really annoying little fault.Read more [javascript:void(0)]Comment|2 people found this helpful. Was this review helpful

[/gp/customer-reviews/R2SE533GWZIYHD/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]Killer sound - keenly priced
[/gp/customer-reviews/R2SE533GWZIYHD/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00YR92VMA]3 August 2016Style: Z333|Verified PurchaseI
had an old set of Logitech multimedia speakers that eventually had the main switch and fader unit fail - had about 9 years use so
not bad. I needed something as a reasonable replacement and not too dear. For the price and specification this set is steal. The
sound quality is excellent at all ranges, there is no hum or interference from PC PSU that can sometimes come through on
inexpensive PC speakers, the bass is responsive and the desktop volume control is very well made. The output is crisp even at the
top end which is VERY loud. Overall its £45 well spent on something very capable of filling my whole 2 bed flat with quality music
should I be that inconsiderate to my neighbours. Fortunately I'm not...Read more [javascript:void(0)]Comment|3 people found this
helpful. Was this review helpful to you? Yes

ABOUT LOGITECH G27
Racing wheel and pedal sets are a popular accessory for players that enjoy motor racing video games, and the Logitech G27 is
designed to replicate the real-life driving experience with a number of features that would be found in a regular car. This
particular model is targeted at PC and PS3 owners, and it comes as three separate units - the wheel and steering column, the gear
shift and pedals. Materials such as Stainless Steel, bearings and leather have been used in the design to make the whole setup
long-lasting. While traditional steering wheel products have always handled like a regular joystick, the Logitech G27 includes
force feedback, and this provides resistance for the steering wheel to replicate the feeling of tyres losing grip on the road. RPM
indicator LED lights allow experienced video game drivers to have full control over gear shift changes when driving in manual
mode, and this can help players to gain a vital speed advantage during a race. As the Logitech G27 comes in three distinct pieces,
accessories are available that allow owners to arrange the parts so that the arrangement is laid out like a real car. Stands make
it easier to choose a left-hand drive or right-hand layout, and custom pedal modifications can also be found that give a more
realistic feeling when pressing down on the accelerator, clutch and brake. For the dedicated video game racing enthusiast,
complete solutions are available, including a racing chair and stand - this provides a complete internal vehicle environment.
